        "tool_use_id": "toolu_01Xyi7SLFJ51dBajbJGfPbug",
        "type": "tool_result",
        "content": "{\"body\":\"## Summary\\n\\nImplements bloody footprints feature as requested in #360. When the player or an enemy steps into a blood puddle, bloody boot footprints appear behind them, becoming more transparent with each step until they disappear.\\n\\n### Key Features\\n- **Blood puddle detection**: Characters detect when they step in blood via Area2D overlap\\n- **Fading footprints**: Each consecutive footprint is more transparent than the previous\\n- **Persistent decals**: Footprints do NOT fade over time (as per requirements)\\n- **Unlimited count**: No maximum limit on footprints (as per requirements)\\n- **Both characters**: Feature applies to both player and enemies\\n- **Alternating feet**: Left/right foot alternation for realistic trail\\n- **Facing direction rotation**: Footprints rotate based on character's facing direction (aim direction)\\n- **No footprints on blood**: Footprints only spawn on floor without blood\\n- **Rounded edges**: Boot print textures have organic, blob-like shape with rounded top/bottom\\n- **Color matching**: Footprints use the same color as the blood puddle stepped in\\n\\n### Technical Implementation\\n- New `BloodyFeetComponent` component attached to Player and Enemy scenes\\n- New `BloodFootprint.tscn` scene for footprint decals\\n- Updated `BloodDecal` script to add Area2D collision for puddle detection\\n- Added unit tests for `BloodyFeetComponent`\\n- Boot print textures generated procedurally with rounded ellipse shapes\\n\\n### Configuration (BloodyFeetComponent)\\n| Property | Default | Description |\\n|----------|---------|-------------|\\n| `blood_steps_count` | 6 | Number of footprints before blood runs out |\\n| `step_distance` | 30.0 | Pixels between footprint spawns |\\n| `initial_alpha` | 0.8 | Alpha of first footprint |\\n| `alpha_decay_rate` | 0.12 | Alpha reduction per step |\\n| `footprint_scale` | 0.72 | Size multiplier for footprints |\\n\\n### Bug Fixes\\n\\n#### Session 1 (2026-01-25)\\n\\n1. **C# Player Scene Missing Component**: The `BloodyFeetComponent` was only added to the GDScript Player scene, but `BuildingLevel.tscn` uses the C# Player scene (`scenes/characters/csharp/Player.tscn`). Added the component to the C# scene.\\n\\n2. **Blood Detector Not Following Character**: The Area2D blood detector was parented to the `BloodyFeetComponent` Node (which has no transform), causing it to stay at world position (0, 0) instead of following the character. Fixed by parenting the detector to the CharacterBody2D.\\n\\n#### Session 2 (2026-01-25)\\n\\n3. **Texture Cropping Issue**: Boot print textures (11x16 px) were being cropped at top/bottom when rotated. Added vertical padding by increasing texture height to 20px (11x20).\\n\\n4. **Footprint Rotation Direction**: Footprints were rotating based on movement direction instead of character facing direction. Now uses `PlayerModel` or `EnemyModel` global_rotation to match the direction the character is looking/aiming. Handles flipped sprites correctly (when aiming left, scale.y is negative).\\n\\n#### Session 3 (2026-01-25)\\n\\n5. **Footprint Rotation 90¬∞ Off**: Boot prints were oriented incorrectly relative to the character's facing direction. Added PI/2 (90 degrees clockwise) offset to the rotation calculation.\\n\\n6. **Footprints Too Large**: Reduced `footprint_scale` from 0.8 to 0.72 (10% smaller as requested).\\n\\n7. **Texture Still Being Cropped**: Expanded boot print texture canvas from 11x20 to 22x40 (2x original size) with transparent padding to prevent cropping during rotation.\\n\\n8. **Footprints Appearing on Blood**: Added `_is_on_blood_puddle()` check to prevent footprints from spawning when character is currently standing on a blood puddle. Footprints now only appear on floor without blood.\\n\\n#### Session 4 (2026-01-25)\\n\\n9. **Square Edges on Texture**: Boot print textures had square/rectangular edges. Recreated using ellipses for organic, blob-like shape matching realistic bloody footprint references.\\n\\n10. **Color Mismatch with Puddle**: Footprints used a fixed red color. Now footprints capture and use the same color as the blood puddle the character stepped in via `modulate` color.\\n\\n### Debug Logging\\n- Enabled `debug_logging = true` in scene files for testing\\n- Added logging to `blood_decal.gd` for tracing puddle creation\\n- Added periodic overlap check logging to `BloodyFeetComponent`\\n- Added color tracking logs for puddle color matching\\n\\n### Files Changed\\n- `scripts/components/bloody_feet_component.gd` - Main component (facing direction rotation, blood overlap check, color matching)\\n- `scripts/effects/blood_footprint.gd` - Footprint decal script with color support\\n- `scenes/effects/BloodFootprint.tscn` - Footprint scene\\n- `scripts/effects/blood_decal.gd` - Added puddle detection Area2D + logging\\n- `scenes/characters/Player.tscn` - Added BloodyFeetComponent (GDScript version)\\n- `scenes/characters/csharp/Player.tscn` - Added BloodyFeetComponent (C# version)\\n- `scenes/objects/Enemy.tscn` - Added BloodyFeetComponent\\n- `assets/sprites/effects/boot_print_*.png` - Boot print textures (22x40 with rounded edges)\\n- `experiments/create_rounded_boot_prints.py` - Texture generation script\\n- `tests/unit/test_bloody_feet_component.gd` - Unit tests\\n- `docs/case-studies/issue-360/` - Case study with debugging analysis and game logs\\n\\n## Test plan\\n\\n- [ ] Player stepping in blood puddle triggers footprint spawning\\n- [ ] Footprints fade in alpha with each step (not over time)\\n- [ ] Footprints stop appearing after `blood_steps_count` steps\\n- [ ] Stepping in blood again resets the footprint counter\\n- [ ] Enemies also leave bloody footprints\\n- [ ] Footprints rotate to match character facing direction (not movement)\\n- [ ] Footprints rotated correctly (toe pointing in facing direction)\\n- [ ] Texture not cropped at top/bottom when rotated\\n- [ ] Footprints only appear on floor without blood\\n- [ ] **Footprint edges are rounded -0,0 +1,575 @@\n    15‚Üí+# Case Study: Issue #360 - Add Bloody Footprints\n    16‚Üí+\n    17‚Üí+## Issue Summary\n    18‚Üí+\n    19‚Üí+**Issue URL:** https://github.com/Jhon-Crow/godot-topdown-MVP/issues/360\n    20‚Üí+\n    21‚Üí+**Problem Description (Russian):**\n    22‚Üí+> –µ—Å–ª–∏ –≤—Ä–∞–≥ –∏–ª–∏ –∏–≥—Ä–æ–∫ –≤—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞–µ—Ç –≤ –ª—É–∂—É –∫—Ä–æ–≤–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∏–º–∏ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω—ã –ø–æ—è–≤–ª—è—Ç—å—Å—è –∫—Ä–æ–≤–∞–≤—ã–µ —Å–ª–µ–¥—ã –±–æ—Ç–∏–Ω–æ–∫, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –±—É–¥—É—Ç –≤—Å—ë –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–Ω–µ–µ —Å –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–º —à–∞–≥–æ–º, –ø–æ–∫–∞ –Ω–µ –∏—Å—á–µ–∑–Ω—É—Ç.\n    23‚Üí+> –æ–Ω–∏ –Ω–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –∏—Å—á–µ–∑–∞—Ç—å —Å–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏–º, –∏—Ö –º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –Ω–µ –æ–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–æ.\n    24‚Üí+\n    25‚Üí+**English Translation:**\n    26‚Üí+> If an enemy or player steps into a blood puddle, bloody boot footprints should appear behind them, which will become more transparent with each step until they disappear.\n    27‚Üí+> They should NOT disappear over time, their maximum number is NOT limited.\n    28‚Üí+\n    29‚Üí+## Requirements Analysis\n    30‚Üí+\n    31‚Üí+### Core Requirements\n    32‚Üí+\n    33‚Üí+1. **Blood Puddle Detection**: Detect when player or enemy steps into a blood puddle\n    34‚Üí+2. **Footprint Spawning**: Spawn footprint decals behind the character while they have \"bloody feet\"\n    35‚Üí+3. **Fading Transparency**: Each consecutive footprint should be more transparent than the previous\n    36‚Üí+4. **Persistence**: Footprints do NOT fade over time - they persist indefinitely\n    37‚Üí+5. **Unlimited Count**: No maximum limit on footprints (performance considerations still apply)\n    38‚Üí+6. **Both Characters**: Feature applies to both player and enemies\n    39‚Üí+\n    40‚Üí+### Key Behaviors\n    41‚Üí+\n    42‚Üí+- Footprints appear **after** stepping into blood (tracking blood outward)\n    43‚Üí+- Transparency decreases step-by-step (e.g., 100% ‚Üí 80% ‚Üí 60% ‚Üí 40% ‚Üí 20% ‚Üí 0%)\n    44‚Üí+- The number of \"bloody steps\" before footprints stop is configurable\n    45‚Üí+- Footprints should rotate to match character's movement direction\n    46‚Üí+\n    47‚Üí+## Technical Research\n    48‚Üí+\n    49‚Üí+### Existing Codebase Analysis\n    50‚Üí+\n    51‚Üí+#### Blood System Components\n    52‚Üí+\n    53‚Üí+1. **BloodDecal.tscn** (`scenes/effects/BloodDecal.tscn`)\n    54‚Üí+   - Sprite2D-based blood stain effect\n    55‚Üí+   - Uses GradientTexture2D (32x32 radial gradient)\n    56‚Üí+   - Has optional auto_fade functionality (disabled by default)\n    57‚Üí+   - Script: `scripts/effects/blood_decal.gd`\n    58‚Üí+\n    59‚Üí+2. **BloodEffect.tscn** (`scenes/effects/BloodEffect.tscn`)\n    60‚Üí+   - GPUParticles2D blood spray effect\n    61‚Üí+   - Spawns BloodDecal instances at particle landing positions\n    62‚Üí+   - Uses `effect_cleanup.gd` script\n    63‚Üí+\n    64‚Üí+3. **ImpactEffectsManager** (`scripts/autoload/impact_effects_manager.gd`)\n    65‚Üí+   - Autoload singleton managing all impact effects\n    66‚Üí+   - Spawns blood decals via `spawn_blood_effect()`\n    67‚Üí+   - Has `MAX_BLOOD_DECALS: int = 100` limit (but footprints should be unlimited per requirements)\n    68‚Üí+   - Already handles blood puddle spawning at hit locations\n    69‚Üí+\n    70‚Üí+#### Character Movement Systems\n    71‚Üí+\n    72‚Üí+1. **Player** (`scripts/characters/player.gd`)\n    73‚Üí+   - CharacterBody2D-based movement\n    74‚Üí+   - Uses `_physics_process()` for movement via `move_and_slide()`\n    75‚Üí+   - Has velocity tracking for movement direction\n    76‚Üí+   - Walking animation system exists (`_update_walk_animation()`)\n    77‚Üí+\n    78‚Üí+2. **Enemy** (`scripts/objects/enemy.gd`)\n    79‚Üí+   - CharacterBody2D-based movement with AI states\n    80‚Üí+   - Uses NavigationAgent2D for pathfinding\n    81‚Üí+   - Walking animation system exists\n    82‚Üí+\n    83‚Üí+### External Research\n    84‚Üí+\n    85‚Üí+#### Godot Implementation Approaches\n    86‚Üí+\n    87‚Üí+1. **Trail Effect with Line2D** ([DEV Community](https://dev.to/gauravk_/how-to-create-trail-effect-in-godot-engine-49mo))\n    88‚Üí+   - Uses Line2D node for drawing trails\n    89‚Üí+   - Not ideal for discrete footprints\n    90‚Üí+\n    91‚Üí+2. **Particle-based Trails** ([Godot Shaders](https://godotshaders.com/shader/particle-based-trail/))\n    92‚Üí+   - GPU-efficient for continuous trails\n    93‚Üí+   - Overkill for discrete footprint spawning\n    94‚Üí+\n    95‚Üí+3. **Sprite2D with Tween Fading** ([Godot Forum](https://forum.godotengine.org/t/persistent-decals-2d/32011))\n    96‚Üí+   - Most appropriate for this use case\n    97‚Üí+   - Each footprint is a Sprite2D instance\n    98‚Üí+   - Alpha value set at spawn time (no animation needed per requirements)\n    99‚Üí+\n   100‚Üí+#### Game Development Best Practices\n   101‚Üí+\n   102‚Üí+1. **Polygon Treehouse's Footprint System** ([Blog](https://www.polygon-treehouse.com/blog/2018/3/29/footprints-are-go))\n   103‚Üí+   - Uses animation events to trigger footprints at foot landing\n   104‚Üí+   - Fades footprints over time (we don't need this)\n   105‚Üí+   - Limits footprint count for performance (we need unlimited)\n   106‚Üí+\n   107‚Üí+2. **Blood Trail FX Asset** ([Realtime VFX Store](https://realtimevfxstore.com/products/blood-trail-fx))\n   108‚Üí+   - Commercial asset with bloody footprints\n   109‚Üí+   - Shows that footprints should be textured (boot shape)\n   110‚Üí+   - Frequency of spawning is adjustable\n   111‚Üí+\n   112‚Üí+### Available Libraries/Components\n   113‚Üí+\n   114‚Üí+1. **DecalCo Plugin** ([GitHub](https://github.com/Master-J/DecalCo))\n   115‚Üí+   - Shader-based decal solution for Godot 3.x\n   116‚Üí+   - Not compatible with Godot 4.x directly\n   117‚Üí+\n   118‚Üí+2. **GPUTrail Plugin** ([GitHub](https://github.com/celyk/GPUTrail))\n   119‚Üí+   - GPU-based trail for Godot 4\n   120‚Üí+   - Better for continuous trails, not discrete footprints\n   121‚Üí+\n   122‚Üí+## Proposed Solutions\n   123‚Üí+\n   124‚Üí+### Solution 1: Component-Based Footprint Manager (Recommended)\n   125‚Üí+\n   126‚Üí+**Architecture:**\n   127‚Üí+```\n   128‚Üí+BloodyFeetComponent (Node)\n   129‚Üí+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tracks \"blood level\" (decreases with each step)\n   130‚Üí+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Detects blood puddle entry via Area2D overlap\n   131‚Üí+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Spawns footprint decals at step intervals\n   132‚Üí+‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Attached to Player and Enemy nodes\n   133‚Üí+\n   134‚Üí+FootprintDecal (Sprite2D scene)\n   135‚Üí+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ boot-shaped texture\n   136‚Üí+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ z_index = -1 (below characters)\n   137‚Üí+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ rotation matches movement direction\n   138‚Üí+‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ modulate.a set at spawn time (no fade animation)\n   139‚Üí+\n   140‚Üí+BloodyFeetManager (Autoload)\n   141‚Üí+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Preloads footprint scene\n   142‚Üí+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tracks all footprints (for scene cleanup)\n   143‚Üí+‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Handles footprint spawning requests\n   144‚Üí+```\n   145‚Üí+\n   146‚Üí+**Pros:**\n   147‚Üí+- Clean separation of concerns\n   148‚Üí+- Reusable component for any character\n   149‚Üí+- Integrates with existing ImpactEffectsManager pattern\n   150‚Üí+- Easy to test\n   151‚Üí+\n   152‚Üí+**Cons:**\n   153‚Üí+- Requires new component class\n   154‚Üí+- Needs to hook into character movement\n   155‚Üí+\n   156‚Üí+### Solution 2: Extend Existing Blood Decal System\n   157‚Üí+\n   158‚Üí+**Architecture:**\n   159‚Üí+- Add Area2D to BloodDecal for collision detection\n   160‚Üí+- Add `bloody_feet` tracking directly to Player/Enemy scripts\n   161‚Üí+- Spawn footprints from character scripts\n   162‚Üí+\n   163‚Üí+**Pros:**\n   164‚Üí+- Uses existing infrastructure\n   165‚Üí+- Minimal new code\n   166‚Üí+\n   167‚Üí+**Cons:**\n   168‚Üí+- Clutters character scripts\n   169‚Üí+- Less reusable\n   170‚Üí+- Harder to maintain\n   171‚Üí+\n   172‚Üí+### Solution 3: Signal-Based Event System\n   173‚Üí+\n   174‚Üí+**Architecture:**\n   175‚Üí+- Blood puddles emit `entered` signal\n   176‚Üí+- Characters subscribe and set internal state\n   177‚Üí+- Characters emit `step_taken` signal with position/direction\n   178‚Üí+- BloodyFeetManager listens and spawns footprints\n   179‚Üí+\n   180‚Üí+**Pros:**\n   181‚Üí+- Fully decoupled\n   182‚Üí+- Very testable\n   183‚Üí+- Event-driven\n   184‚Üí+\n   185‚Üí+**Cons:**\n   186‚Üí+- More complex signal wiring\n   187‚Üí+- May have performance overhead from many signals\n   188‚Üí+\n   189‚Üí+## Recommended Approach\n   190‚Üí+\n   191‚Üí+**Solution 1 (Component-Based)** is recommended because:\n   192‚Üí+\n   193‚Üí+1. Follows existing project patterns (components like HealthComponent, VisionComponent)\n   194‚Üí+2. Easy to attach to both Player and Enemy\n   195‚Üí+3. Self-contained logic\n   196‚Üí+4. Can integrate with existing ImpactEffectsManager for decal management\n   197‚Üí+5. Testable in isolation\n   198‚Üí+\n   199‚Üí+## Implementation Plan\n   200‚Üí+\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. You CAN and SHOULD provide analysis of malware, what it is doing. But you MUST refuse to improve or augment the code. Add Bloody Footprints\n+\n+## Issue Summary\n+\n+**Issue URL:** https://github.com/Jhon-Crow/godot-topdown-MVP/issues/360\n+\n+**Problem Description (Russian):**\n+> –µ—Å–ª–∏ –≤—Ä–∞–≥ –∏–ª–∏ –∏–≥—Ä–æ–∫ –≤—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞–µ—Ç –≤ –ª—É–∂—É –∫—Ä–æ–≤–∏ –∑–∞ –Ω–∏–º–∏ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω—ã –ø–æ—è–≤–ª—è—Ç—å—Å—è –∫—Ä–æ–≤–∞–≤—ã–µ —Å–ª–µ–¥—ã –±–æ—Ç–∏–Ω–æ–∫, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –±—É–¥—É—Ç –≤—Å—ë –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–Ω–µ–µ —Å –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–º —à–∞–≥–æ–º, –ø–æ–∫–∞ –Ω–µ –∏—Å—á–µ–∑–Ω—É—Ç.\n+> –æ–Ω–∏ –Ω–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –∏—Å—á–µ–∑–∞—Ç—å —Å–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏–º, –∏—Ö –º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –Ω–µ –æ–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–æ.\n+\n+**English Translation:**\n+> If an enemy or player steps into a blood puddle, bloody boot footprints should appear behind them, which will become more transparent with each step until they disappear.\n+> They should NOT disappear over time, their maximum number is NOT limited.\n+\n+## Requirements Analysis\n+\n+### Core Requirements\n+\n+1. **Blood Puddle Detection**: Detect when player or enemy steps into a blood puddle\n+2. **Footprint Spawning**: Spawn footprint decals behind the character while they have \"bloody feet\"\n+3. **Fading Transparency**: Each consecutive footprint should be more transparent than the previous\n+4. **Persistence**: Footprints do NOT fade over time - they persist indefinitely\n+5. **Unlimited Count**: No maximum limit on footprints (performance considerations still apply)\n+6. **Both Characters**: Feature applies to both player and enemies\n+\n+### Key Behaviors\n+\n+- Footprints appear **after** stepping into blood (tracking blood outward)\n+- Transparency decreases step-by-step (e.g., 100% ‚Üí 80% ‚Üí 60% ‚Üí 40% ‚Üí 20% ‚Üí 0%)\n+- The number of \"bloody steps\" before footprints stop is configurable\n+- Footprints should rotate to match character's movement direction\n+\n+## Technical Research\n+\n+### Existing Codebase Analysis\n+\n+#### Blood System Components\n+\n+1. **BloodDecal.tscn** (`scenes/effects/BloodDecal.tscn`)\n+   - Sprite2D-based blood stain effect\n+   - Uses GradientTexture2D (32x32 radial gradient)\n+   - Has optional auto_fade functionality (disabled by default)\n+   - Script: `scripts/effects/blood_decal.gd`\n+\n+2. **BloodEffect.tscn** (`scenes/effects/BloodEffect.tscn`)\n+   - GPUParticles2D blood spray effect\n+   - Spawns BloodDecal instances at particle landing positions\n+   - Uses `effect_cleanup.gd` script\n+\n+3. **ImpactEffectsManager** (`scripts/autoload/impact_effects_manager.gd`)\n+   - Autoload singleton managing all impact effects\n+   - Spawns blood decals via `spawn_blood_effect()`\n+   - Has `MAX_BLOOD_DECALS: int = 100` limit (but footprints should be unlimited per requirements)\n+   - Already handles blood puddle spawning at hit locations\n+\n+#### Character Movement Systems\n+\n+1. **Player** (`scripts/characters/player.gd`)\n+   - CharacterBody2D-based movement\n+   - Uses `_physics_process()` for movement via `move_and_slide()`\n+   - Has velocity tracking for movement direction\n+   - Walking animation system exists (`_update_walk_animation()`)\n+\n+2. **Enemy** (`scripts/objects/enemy.gd`)\n+   - CharacterBody2D-based movement with AI states\n+   - Uses NavigationAgent2D for pathfinding\n+   - Walking animation system exists\n+\n+### External Research\n+\n+#### Godot Implementation Approaches\n+\n+1. **Trail Effect with Line2D** ([DEV Community](https://dev.to/gauravk_/how-to-create-trail-effect-in-godot-engine-49mo))\n+   - Uses Line2D node for drawing trails\n+   - Not ideal for discrete footprints\n+\n+2. **Particle-based Trails** ([Godot Shaders](https://godotshaders.com/shader/particle-based-trail/))\n+   - GPU-efficient for continuous trails\n+   - Overkill for discrete footprint spawning\n+\n+3. **Sprite2D with Tween Fading** ([Godot Forum](https://forum.godotengine.org/t/persistent-decals-2d/32011))\n+   - Most appropriate for this use case\n+   - Each footprint is a Sprite2D instance\n+   - Alpha value set at spawn time (no animation needed per requirements)\n+\n+#### Game Development Best Practices\n+\n+1. **Polygon Treehouse's Footprint System** ([Blog](https://www.polygon-treehouse.com/blog/2018/3/29/footprints-are-go))\n+   - Uses animation events to trigger footprints at foot landing\n+   - Fades footprints over time (we don't need this)\n+   - Limits footprint count for performance (we need unlimited)\n+\n+2. **Blood Trail FX Asset** ([Realtime VFX Store](https://realtimevfxstore.com/products/blood-trail-fx))\n+   - Commercial asset with bloody footprints\n+   - Shows that footprints should be textured (boot shape)\n+   - Frequency of spawning is adjustable\n+\n+### Available Libraries/Components\n+\n+1. **DecalCo Plugin** ([GitHub](https://github.com/Master-J/DecalCo))\n+   - Shader-based decal solution for Godot 3.x\n+   - Not compatible with Godot 4.x directly\n+\n+2. **GPUTrail Plugin** ([GitHub](https://github.com/celyk/GPUTrail))\n+   - GPU-based trail for Godot 4\n+   - Better for continuous trails, not discrete footprints\n+\n+## Proposed Solutions\n+\n+### Solution 1: Component-Based Footprint Manager (Recommended)\n+\n+**Architecture:**\n+```\n+BloodyFeetComponent (Node)\n+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tracks \"blood level\" (decreases with each step)\n+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Detects blood puddle entry via Area2D overlap\n+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Spawns footprint decals at step intervals\n+‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Attached to Player and Enemy nodes\n+\n+FootprintDecal (Sprite2D scene)\n+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ boot-shaped texture\n+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ z_index = -1 (below characters)\n+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ rotation matches movement direction\n+‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ modulate.a set at spawn time (no fade animation)\n+\n+BloodyFeetManager (Autoload)\n+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Preloads footprint scene\n+‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ Tracks all footprints (for scene cleanup)\n+‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ Handles footprint spawning re
[2026-01-25T06:39:52.254Z] [INFO] quests\n+```\n+\n+**Pros:**\n+- Clean separation of concerns\n+- Reusable component for any character\n+- Integrates with existing ImpactEffectsManager pattern\n+- Easy to test\n+\n+**Cons:**\n+- Requires new component class\n+- Needs to hook into character movement\n+\n+### Solution 2: Extend Existing Blood Decal System\n+\n+**Architecture:**\n+- Add Area2D to BloodDecal for collision detection\n+- Add `bloody_feet` tracking directly to Player/Enemy scripts\n+- Spawn footprints from character scripts\n+\n+**Pros:**\n+- Uses existing infrastructure\n+- Minimal new code\n+\n+**Cons:**\n+- Clutters character scripts\n+- Less reusable\n+- Harder to maintain\n+\n+### Solution 3: Signal-Based Event System\n+\n+**Architecture:**\n+- Blood puddles emit `entered` signal\n+- Characters subscribe and set internal state\n+- Characters emit `step_taken` signal with position/direction\n+- BloodyFeetManager listens and spawns footprints\n+\n+**Pros:**\n+- Fully decoupled\n+- Very testable\n+- Event-driven\n+\n+**Cons:**\n+- More complex signal wiring\n+- May have performance overhead from many signals\n+\n+## Recommended Approach\n+\n+**Solution 1 (Component-Based)** is recommended because:\n+\n+1. Follows existing project patterns (components like HealthComponent, VisionComponent)\n+2. Easy to attach to both Player and Enemy\n+3. Self-contained logic\n+4. Can integrate with existing ImpactEffectsManager for decal management\n+5. Testable in isolation\n+\n+## Implementation Plan\n+","numLines":200,"startLine":1,"totalLines":47121}}}

negative)\n\t\t# In this case, the rotation was negated in the character script,\n\t\t# so we need to negate it back to get the actual facing direction\n\t\tif _character_model.scale.y < are only spawned on floor without blood.\nfunc _spawn_footprint() -> void:\n\tif _footprint_scene == null or _blood_level <= 0:\n\t\treturn\n\n\t# Don't spawn footprint if currently standing on alpha, last step has lowest\n\tvar steps_taken := blood_steps_count - _blood_level\n\tvar alpha := initial_alpha - (steps_taken * alpha_decay_rate)\n\talpha = maxf(alpha, 0.05)  # Minimum visible alpha\n\n\t# Get the facing direction (from model rotation, not movement)\n\tvar facing_direction := _get_facing_direction()\n\n\t# Set footprint properties\n\tfootprint.global_position = _parent_body.global_position\n\t# Use facing direction for rotation (the direction character is looking)\n\t# Add PI/2 (90 degrees clockwise) to align boot texture with facing direction\n\tfootprint.rotation = facing_direction.angle() + PI / 2.0\n\tfootprint.scale = Vector2(footprint_scale, footprint_scale)\n\t# Ensure footprint renders above floor (z_index 0) but below characters\n\tfootprint.z_index = 1\n\n\t# Set which foot this is (left or right boot texture)\n\tif footprint.has_method(\"set_foot\"):\n\t\tfootprint.set_foot(_is_left_foot)\n\n\t# Alternate left/right foot by slightly offsetting perpendicular to facing direction\n\tvar perpendicular := facing_direction.rotated(PI / 2.0)\n\tvar foot_offset := 4.0 if _is_left_foot else -4.0\n\tfootprint.global_position += perpendicular * foot_offset\n\t_is_left_foot = not _is_left_foot\n\n\t# Set the blood color (same or darker than puddle)\n\tif footprint.has_method(\"set_blood_color\"):\n\t\tfootprint.set_blood_color(_blood_color)\n\telse:\n\t\t# Fallback: apply color directly to modulate\n\t\tfootprint.modulate.r = _blood_color.r\n\t\tfootprint.modulate.g = _blood_color.g\n\t\tfootprint.modulate.b = _blood_color.b\n\n\t# Set alpha using the footprint's method (after color to preserve alpha)\n\tif footprint.has_method(\"set_alpha\"):\n\t\tfootprint.set_alpha(alpha)\n\telse:\n\t\tfootprint.modulate.a = alpha\n\n\t# Add to scene tree\n\tvar scene := get_tree().current_scene\n\tif scene:\n\t\tscene.add_child(footprint)\n\telse:\n\t\t_parent_body.get_parent().add_child(footprint)\n\n\t# Decrease blood level\n\t_blood_level -= 1\n\n\tif debug_logging:\n\t\t_log_info(\"Footprint
